###########################
# Annexation Events concerning Asia & Oceania
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

# Table of Contents
#	This might sound arcane to you, but we are folliwng a center-west-north-east-south route. You'll get the hang of it
#
# Central Asia
#	Central Asia
#		Alash
#		Turkestan
#			Bukhara
#			Khiva
#	Afghanistan
#
# Northern Asia
#	Siberia
#	Far Eastern Russia
#
# Eastern Asia
#	China
#		Tibet
#		Xinjiang
#		Mongolia
#			Tuva
#		Manchuria
#		Legation Cities
#	Korea
#	Japan
#		Sakhalin
#	Taiwan
#
# South-East Asia
#	Siam
#	Indochina
#		Vietnam
#		Laos
#		Cambodia
#	Philippines
#	Indonesia
#	Papua New Guinea
#	Malaysia
#		Sarawak
#
# South Asia
#	India
#		Central India
#		Maharashtra
#		Gujarat
#		Rajputana
#		Khalistan
#		Kashmir
#		Sikkim
#		Assam
#		Bengal
#		Orissa
#		Chhatisgarh
#		Vizagapatnam
#		Hyderabad
#		Andhra
#		Madras
#		Mysore
#	Pakistan // Punjab
#		Baluchistan
#		Quetta
#		Sindh
#	Nepal
#	Bhutan
#	Burma
#		Kachin
#		Shan
#	Ceylon
#
# Oceania
#	Australia
#	New Zealand
#	Hawaii

add_namespace = annex

#####################################
##     C E N T R A L   A S I A     ##
#####################################

country_event = { #Fate of Central Asia
	id = annex.3000
	title = annexation_CA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CA_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_alash = no }
				remove_claim_by = ALO
				remove_core_of = ALO
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_turkestan = no }
				remove_claim_by = TRK
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_bukhara = no }
				remove_claim_by = BUK
				remove_core_of = BUK
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_khiva = no }
				remove_claim_by = KHI
				remove_core_of = KHI
			}
			TRK = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Liberate an united Central Asia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3000 option annex.3000.a"
		name = annex.3000.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:571.owner = { #Omsk
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_central_asia = yes
				NOT = {
					is_claimed_by = var:tag_to_release
					is_core_of = var:tag_to_release
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = TRK
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		var:tag_to_release = { set_cosmetic_tag = CA_united }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3000 option annex.3000.b"
		name = annex.3000.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			var:571.owner = { #Omsk
				is_russian_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 571.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_central_asia = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #divide
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3000 option annex.3000.c"
		name = annex.3000.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:571.owner = { #Omsk
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = CA_CONQ days = 100 value = 1 }
		recheck_annexations_immediate = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3000 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_central_asia = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
					owner = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3000 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = CA_CONQ
		set_country_flag = ALO_CONQ
		set_country_flag = TRK_CONQ
		set_country_flag = BUK_CONQ
		set_country_flag = KHI_CONQ
		occupy_massive_country = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Alash
	id = annex.3001
	title = annexation_ALO_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ALO_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_alash = no }
				remove_claim_by = ALO
				remove_core_of = ALO
			}
			ALO = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.3001.a"
		name = annex.3001.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_central_asian_tag = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = BUK }
					OR = {
						owns_state = 407 #Tashkent
						owns_state = 712 #Kyzylkum
						owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:571.owner = { #Omsk
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				TRK = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					has_cosmetic_tag = CA_united
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.3001.b"
		name = annex.3001.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			var:571.owner = { #Omsk
				is_russian_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 571.owner }
		ALO = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Turkestan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.3001.c"
		name = annex.3001.c
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			TRK = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:571.owner = { #Omsk
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		ALO = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory_and_add_claims = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				is_central_asian_tag = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = BUK }
				OR = {
					owns_state = 407 #Tashkent
					owns_state = 712 #Kyzylkum
					owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_alash = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
					owner = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3001 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = ALO_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Bukhara
	id = annex.3003
	title = annexation_BUK_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BUK_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_bukhara = no }
				remove_claim_by = BUK
				remove_core_of = BUK
			}
			BUK = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.3003.a"
		name = annex.3003.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_central_asian_tag = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = ALO }
					OR = {
						owns_state = 407 #Tashkent
						owns_state = 712 #Kyzylkum
						owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					var:407.owner = { #Tashkent
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					var:861.owner = { #Khorezm
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				TRK = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
						has_cosmetic_tag = CA_united
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BUK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.3003.b"
		name = annex.3003.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			OR = {
				var:407.owner = { #Tashkent
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				var:861.owner = { #Khorezm
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:407.owner = { #Tashkent
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 407.owner }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 861.owner }
		}
		BUK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Turkestan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.3003.c"
		name = annex.3003.c
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			TRK = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					var:407.owner = { #Tashkent
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					var:861.owner = { #Khorezm
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		BUK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory_and_add_claims = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Alash
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.3003.d"
		name = annex.3003.d
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
			ALO = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
				OR = {
					owns_state = 407 #Tashkent
					owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					var:407.owner = { #Tashkent
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					var:861.owner = { #Khorezm
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
		BUK = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory_and_add_claims = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				is_central_asian_tag = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ALO }
				OR = {
					owns_state = 407 #Tashkent
					owns_state = 712 #Kyzylkum
					owns_state = 861 #Khorezm
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_bukhara = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
					owner = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3003 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			is_central_asian_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = BUK_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

	id = annex.3004
	title = annexation_KHI_CONQ

	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_scenery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_khiva = no }
				remove_claim_by = KHI
				remove_core_of = KHI
			}
			KHI = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}

	option = { #Liberate

				}
			}

				factor = 0

					var:587.owner = { #Mangyshlak
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					var:712.owner = { #Kyzylkum
						is_russian_tag = yes

					}

				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
		}

			limit = {
				var:587.owner = { #Mangyshlak
					is_russian_tag = yes

country_event = { #Fate of Siberia
	id = annex.3008
	title = annexation_SIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SIB_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = SIB } }
				add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = SIB }
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			}
			537 = { retain_state = yes } #Sakhalin
			555 = { retain_state = yes } #Kuril Islands
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3008 option annex.3008.a"
		name = annex.3008.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = SIB }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					TRM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					RUS = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_siberia = yes
						AND = {
							is_russian_far_east = yes
							country_exists = TRM
							NOT = { TRM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes } }
						}
						AND = {
							is_russian_far_east = yes
							ROOT = { has_country_flag = TRM_CONQ }
							is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = SIB
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3008 option annex.3008.c"
		name = annex.3008.c #give it to Russia
		trigger = {
			RUS = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 300
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				TRM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RUS }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_siberia = yes
						AND = {
							is_russian_far_east = yes
							country_exists = TRM
							NOT = { TRM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes } }
						}
					}
				}
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3008 option annex.3008.d"
		name = annex.3008.d #give it to Transamur
		trigger = {
			TRM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 300 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRM }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_siberia = yes
						is_russian_far_east = yes
					}
				}
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3008 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = SIB_CONQ
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

#####################################

country_event = { #Fate of China
	id = annex.3010
	title = annexation_CHI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CHI_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			determine_chinese_ally = yes
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = LEC }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_claim_by = LEC
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP
					any_owned_state = {
						is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
						is_valid_annexation_state = yes
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = japan_can_annex_coastal_cities
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release China
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3010 option annex.china.release_china"
		name = annex.china.release_china
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_release_target
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = japan_can_annex_coastal_cities
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_release_target }
		release_chinese_government = yes
		var:tag_to_release = { china_puppet_setup = yes }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Release FNG, keep the coastal cities
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3010 option annex.china.release_china_take_coastline"
		name = annex.china.release_china_take_coastline
		trigger = {
			original_tag = JAP
			has_event_target = china_release_target
			has_event_target = japan_can_annex_coastal_cities
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_release_target }
		release_chinese_government = yes
		var:tag_to_release = { china_puppet_setup = yes }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to a Chinese ally
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3010 option annex.china.give_to_china"
		name = annex.china.give_to_china
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
			NOT = { has_event_target = japan_forced_return }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = china_release_target
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = japan_can_annex_coastal_cities
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_ally_target }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					743 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Shanghai
					has_country_flag = LEC_CONQ
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_china_proper = yes
					is_possible_legation_cities_state = no
					is_valid_annexation_state = yes
				}
				transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_china_proper = yes
					is_valid_annexation_state = yes
				}

			}

					NOT = { is_ally_with = TIB }

			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

					region = 146 #Himalayas

					state = 858 #Tawang

					is_core_of = TIB
					state = 353 #Yushu
					state = 601 #Xikang
					state = 858 #Tawang

						state = 604 #Xining
						OR = {
							353 = { is_owned_by = ROOT }

				}
			}

					is_in_faction_with = ENT
					is_american_tag = no
				}
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_conservative
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 10
						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 63
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 3
						national_populist = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = market_liberal
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0

country_event = { #Fate of Japan
	id = annex.3018
	title = annexation_JAP_CONQ
	desc = annexation_JAP_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP_fading_sun = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_russian_tag = yes }
				add_state_claim = 537 #Sakhalin
				add_state_claim = 555 #Kurils
				add_state_claim = 745 #Kwantung
			}
		}
		537 = { retain_state = yes } #Sakhalin
	}

	option = { #Transitional government
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3018 option annex.3018.a"
		name = annex.3018.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JAP }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					is_core_of = JAP
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 630 #Johnston Atoll
							state = 631 #Midway Island
							state = 632 #Wake Island
							state = 638 #Guam
							state = 642 #Phoenix Island
							state = 726 #Samoa
							state = 727 #Line Islands
						}
						629 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Hawaii
						any_of = {
							array = ROOT.faction_members
							NOT = {
								is_core_of = var:v
								is_claimed_by = var:v
							}
						}
						any_of = {
							array = ROOT.subjects
							NOT = {
								is_core_of = var:v
								is_claimed_by = var:v
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_claim_of_target = yes
			transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		JAP_socialist_puppet_effect = yes
		JAP_democratic_puppet_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_state
				load_focus_tree = japan_subject_focus
				if = {
					limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					promote_character = JAP_katayama_tetsu
					promote_character = JAP_ishibashi_tanzan
				}
				JAP_close_all = yes
				JAP_clear_ideas = yes
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = japdom.241 days = 16 random_days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = japdom.240 days = 16 random_days = 7 }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupation
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3018 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = JAP_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Vietnam
	id = annex.3023
	title = annexation_VIN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_VIN_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = JAP }
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = VIN }
					remove_claim_by = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Puppet Vietnam
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3023 option annex.3023.a"
		name = annex.3023.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_subject = GEA }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = VIN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = var:VIN.overlord
				country_exists = INC
				INC = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = INC_Unification }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { INC = { is_subject = yes } }
				var:INC.overlord = { country_event = { id = viet.1955 hours = 8 } }
			}
			else = {
				INC = { country_event = { id = viet.1955 hours = 8 } }
			}
		}
		if = { #Empower the VNQQD
			limit = { china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes }
			VIN_released_by_chi = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to GEA
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3023 option annex.asia.give_to_gea"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_gea

		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		name = annex.3023.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = CAM
				original_tag = SIA
			}
			owns_state = 826 #Stung Treng
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		286 = { #Cochinchina
			retain_state = yes #for the release_targeted_tag tooltip
			add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
				add_resistance = 20
			}
		}
		856 = { #Mekong Delta
			retain_state = yes #for the release_targeted_tag tooltip

				limit = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }

			}

country_event = { #Fate of Indonesia
	id = annex.3027
	title = annexation_INS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_INS_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = DEI }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = DEI }
					remove_core_of = DEI
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = JAP }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = JAP
						is_indonesia = yes
						NOT = {
							state = 333 #North Borneo
							state = 828 #Sabah
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = JAP
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = INS
					OR = {
						is_indonesia = no
						region = 167 #New Guinea
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = INS
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3027 option annex.3027.a"
		name = annex.3027.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_subject = GEA
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INS }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject_of = JAP }
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}

			INS = { country_event = ins.116 } #bring Tan Malaka back
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		trigger = {
			tag = HOL
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { country_exists = DEI }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1000 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DEI }
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = INS }
			add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			hidden_effect = { HOL_DEI_is_restored = yes }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to DEI
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3027 option annex.3027.c"
		name = annex.3027.c
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = {
			DEI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		INS = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DEI }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to HOL
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3027 option annex.3027.d"
		name = annex.3027.d
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = {
			HOL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			HOL = {
				is_subject = no
				has_socialist_government = no
			}

		}
		INS = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		transfer_targeted_territory = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate into GEA
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3027 option annex.asia.give_to_gea"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_gea
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }

			transfer_targeted_territory = yes
		}

country_event = { #Fate of India
	id = annex.3031
	title = annexation_IND_CONQ
	desc = annexation_IND_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = RAJ }
				NOT = { country_exists = PRF }
			}
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;INDIA IS CONQUERED BY FOREIGN POWER;[GetDateText]"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			india_reset_cores_claims = yes
			HND = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			RAJ = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_entente
				every_character = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = HND_character }
					clr_character_flag = HND_character
					set_nationality = HND
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_chinese_tag = yes
					858 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				}
				add_state_claim = 858 #Tawang
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet Indian state
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3031 option annex.3031.a"
		name = annex.3031.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
				AND = {
					original_tag = IMP
					tag = ENT
					NOT = { country_exists = RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					RAJ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					ENT = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HND }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_hindustan = yes }
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_india = yes
					is_hindustan = no
				}
				add_claim_of_target = yes
			}
		}
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		HND_puppet_setup = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #release as British India
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3031 option annex.3031.c"
		name = annex.3031.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = IMP
			tag = ENT
			is_faction_leader = yes
			NOT = { country_exists = RAJ }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = no
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_hindustan = yes }
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_india = yes
					is_hindustan = no
					NOT = { is_core_of = CEY }
				}
				add_claim_of_target = yes
			}
		}
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to the British
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3031 option annex.3039.b"
		name = annex.3039.b
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
				RAJ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			ENT = {
				original_tag = IMP
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ENT }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				is_india = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to the Raj
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3031 option annex.3039.k"
		name = annex.3039.k
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
			RAJ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}

		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		}

			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes

		trigger = {

				tag = RAJ

		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = new_annexation_decisions_tt
		set_country_flag = { flag = IND_CONQ days = 100 value = 1 }
		recheck_annexations_immediate = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3031 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = IND_CONQ
		set_country_flag = ANDHRA_CONQ
		set_country_flag = ASM_CONQ
		set_country_flag = BALUCH_CONQ

country_event = { #Fate of Hindustan // Central India
	id = annex.3032
	title = annexation_HND_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HND_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		439 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			RAJ = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_entente
				every_character = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = HND_character }
					clr_character_flag = HND_character
					set_nationality = HND
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet HND
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3032.a"
		name = annex.3032.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = PRF
				tag = RAJ
				AND = {
					original_tag = IMP
					tag = ENT
					is_faction_leader = yes
					NOT = { country_exists = RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HIN }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_hindustan = yes }
				add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
			}
			#exception: Patiala - owned by HND at game start
			if = {
				limit = {
					815 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Patiala
					440 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #East Punjab
					NOT = { is_ally_with = PAK }
					NOT = { is_ally_with = PJB }
				}
				815 = { add_core_of = var:tag_to_release }
			}
			#exception: Ajmer - owned by HND at game start
			if = {
				limit = {
					839 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Ajmer
					433 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Rajputana
					NOT = { is_ally_with = RJS }
				}
				839 = { add_core_of = var:tag_to_release }
			}
			HND = { clear_cores_of_tag_if_possible = yes }
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #release as British India
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3031.c"
		name = annex.3031.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = IMP
			tag = ENT
			is_faction_leader = yes
			NOT = { country_exists = RAJ }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_hindustan = yes }
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_india = yes
					is_hindustan = no
				}
				add_claim_of_target = yes
				retain_state = yes
			}
		}
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to the British
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3039.b"
		name = annex.3039.b
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
				RAJ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			ENT = {
				original_tag = IMP
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ENT }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_hindustan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to the Raj
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3039.b"
		name = annex.3039.b
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
			RAJ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RAJ }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_hindustan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to PRF
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3039.u"
		name = annex.3039.u
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
			PRF = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PRF }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_hindustan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #incorporate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.3039.f"
		name = annex.3039.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 200 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_hindustan = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3032 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RAJ
				tag = PRF
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = HND_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		430 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
	}

	option = { #puppet BNG
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3040 option annex.3040.a"

		ai_chance = { base = 20 }

		trigger = {

				is_greater_bengal = yes
				is_bengal = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				owns_state = 434 #Manipur
				NOT = { owns_state = 432 } #Assam
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BNG }
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_bengal = yes }
			add_core_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_greater_bengal = yes }
			add_claim_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #release Bharatiya
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3040 option annex.3040.c"
		name = annex.3040.c
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes

				country_exists = HND

				is_bengal = no
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = { is_greater_bengal = yes }
				remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			}

				limit = {
					is_india = yes
					is_greater_bengal = no
				}
				add_claim_of_target = yes
				retain_state = yes
			}
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = KR_Bharatiya_Commune
				keep_completed = yes
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

					is_indian_tag = yes

country_event = { #Fate of Australasia
	id = annex.3058
	title = annexation_AST_CONQ
	desc = annexation_AST_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = AST
				if = {
					limit = { is_australia = yes }
					add_core_of = AST
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = AST
				}
			}
			AST = {
				remove_ideas = {
					AST_british_advisors_idea
					AST_uob_advisors_idea
					AST_anderson_doctrine_idea
					AST_new_guard_military_1
					AST_new_guard_military_2
					AST_new_guard_economy_1
					AST_new_guard_economy_2
					AST_rising_power
					AST_totalist_economy_idea
					AST_AFM_economy_1
					AST_AFM_economy_2
				}
				AST_become_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = GBR
					is_ally_with = GBR
				}
				GBR = { save_event_target_as = british_target }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ENT
					is_ally_with = ENT
					ENT = { is_commonwealth_tag = yes }
				}
				ENT = { save_event_target_as = british_target }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = CAN
					is_ally_with = CAN
					CAN = { CAN_is_dominion = yes }
				}
				CAN = { save_event_target_as = british_target }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				GEA = { country_event = { id = austral.373 days = 20 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Puppet Australasia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.3058.a"
		name = annex.3058.a
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }

			284 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #North Island
			NOT = { has_event_target = british_target }
		}

		AST = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		NZL = { set_transfer_target_cores = yes }
		transfer_targeted_territory_and_add_cores = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 636 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } } #Fiji
				636 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
			}
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		AST_puppet_setup = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Release New Zealand
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.3058.b"
		name = annex.3058.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		trigger = {
			284 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #North Island
			NOT = { has_event_target = british_target }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NZL }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 636 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } } #Fiji
				636 = { add_claim_of_target = yes }
			}
		}
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		NZL_puppet_setup = yes

	}

	option = { #Puppet Australasia and give it the Pacific Islands

			284 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #North Island

				734 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Nauru

		AST_puppet_setup = yes
		AST = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 60
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #return it to ENT
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.3058.g"
		name = annex.3058.g
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = british_target
			NOT = { tag = event_target:british_target }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:british_target }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = AST
					is_claimed_by = AST
					is_core_of = NZL
					is_claimed_by = NZL
					is_core_of = PNG
					state = 636 #Fiji
				}
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_without_overriding_occupation = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3058 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = event_target:british_target
				NOT = { has_event_target = british_target }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = AST_CONQ
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Hawaii
	id = annex.3061
	title = annexation_HAW_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HAW_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = HAW
				if = {
					limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
					add_core_of = HAW
				}
				else = {
					remove_core_of = HAW
				}
			}
			HAW = {
				clr_country_flag = HAW_can_join_factions
				HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa = { remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Hawaii as a republic
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.3061.a"
		name = annex.3061.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				original_tag = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_allied_country = { is_american_tag = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HAW }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_monarchy_restoration
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_completed_focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					has_completed_focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Release Hawaii as a monarchy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.3061.b"
		name = annex.3061.b
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				original_tag = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_allied_country = { is_american_tag = yes }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HAW }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		HAW = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = HAW_kingdom
			HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa = {
				set_character_name = HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa_regnal
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa
					country_leader = { ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa
					country_leader = { ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa
					country_leader = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = HAW_lydia_liliuokalani_kawananakoa
					country_leader = { ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_revolution_succeeds
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = HAW_declare_a_republic }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HAW_declare_a_republic
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to America
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.3061.c"
		name = annex.3061.c
		trigger = {
			var:797.owner = {
				is_american_tag = yes
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				original_tag = JAP
				NOT = { is_ally_with = 797.owner }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 797.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_american_pacific_islands = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to Japan
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.3061.d"
		name = annex.3061.d
		trigger = {
			JAP = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JAP }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_american_pacific_islands = yes
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
			}
			transfer_state_and_notify = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to GEA
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.asia.give_to_gea"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_gea
		trigger = {
			has_subject = GEA

			}

		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3061 option annex.3061.f"
		name = annex.3061.f
		trigger = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				original_tag = JAP
				is_ally_with = 797.owner
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_american_pacific_islands = yes

	}

	option = {

					OR = {
						tag = INC
						tag = GEA
					}
					owns_state = 670 #Laos
				}
				GEA = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 670 #Laos
				}
			}
			SIA = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:670.owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = INC
						tag = LAO
					}
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = SIA }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIA }
		882 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3065 option annex.3065.c"
		name = annex.3065.c #Give to INC
		trigger = {
			INC = {
				owns_state = 670 #Laos
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SIA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				NOT = { is_ally_with = INC }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INC }
		if = {
			limit = {
				670 = { is_core_of = var:tag_to_release } #Laos
			}
			882 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		}
		else = {
			882 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3065 option annex.asia.give_to_gea"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_gea #Give to GEA
		trigger = {
			GEA = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				owns_state = 670 #Laos
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEA }
		882 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3065 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = SIA
				AND = {
					OR = {
						tag = INC
						tag = GEA
					}
					owns_state = 670 #Laos
				}
			}

						tag = INC
						tag = GEA

			}
		}

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	desc = annexation_NORTHERN_MALAYA_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.3067.a"
		name = annex.3067.a #Give to MAL
		trigger = {
			MAL = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				add = -40
				state = 830 #Pattani
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					SIA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					NOT = { is_ally_with = MAL }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAL }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes } #scoped for the tooltip
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.3067.b"
		name = annex.3067.b #Give to SIA
		trigger = {
			SIA = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				state = 830 #Pattani
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						MAL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
						INS = {
							is_ally_with = ROOT
							owns_state = 846 #Johore
						}
						GEA = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							owns_state = 846 #Johore
						}
					}
					NOT = { is_ally_with = SIA }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIA }
		THIS = { #scoped for the tooltip
			if = {
				limit = { state = 830 } #Pattani
				transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
			}
			else = {
				transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.3067.c"
		name = annex.3067.c #Give to INS
		trigger = {
			INS = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
				owns_state = 846 #Johore
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INS }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes } #scoped for the tooltip
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.asia.give_to_gea"
		name = annex.asia.give_to_gea #Give to GEA
		trigger = {
			GEA = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				owns_state = 846 #Johore
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1000 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEA }
		THIS = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes } #scoped for the tooltip
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.integration"
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GEA
					tag = INS
					tag = SIA
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1000 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { tag = SIA }
				state = 830 #Pattani
			}
			owner = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		else = {
			owner = { add_state_claim = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event annex.3067 option annex.occupation"
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SIA
					tag = INS
					tag = GEA
					AND = {
						has_subject = GEA
						GEA = { owns_state = 846 } #Johore
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		if = {
			limit = { state = 751 } #Kelantan-Trengganu
			ROOT = { set_country_flag = KELANTAN_CONQ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { state = 830 } #Pattani
			ROOT = { set_country_flag = PATTANI_CONQ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { state = 999 } #Kedah-Perlis
			ROOT = { set_country_flag = KEDAH_CONQ }
		}
	}
}
